\item 
typedef uint64\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceflatbuffers_a2bdea2ebee948e32359f5598e98a7cd4}{hash\+\_\+value\+\_\+t}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Function types to be used with resolving hashes into objects and back again. The resolver gets a pointer to a field inside an object API object that is of the type specified in the schema using the attribute {\ttfamily cpp\+\_\+type} (it is thus important whatever you write to this address matches that type). The value of this field is initially null, so you may choose to implement a delayed binding lookup using this function if you wish. The resolver does the opposite lookup, for when the object is being serialized again. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
typedef std\+::function$<$ void(void \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}pointer\+\_\+adr, \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceflatbuffers_a2bdea2ebee948e32359f5598e98a7cd4}{hash\+\_\+value\+\_\+t}} hash)$>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceflatbuffers_ac7bfda6e698d13cd1b225df198a24a18}{resolver\+\_\+function\+\_\+t}}

\Hypertarget{namespaceflatbuffers_a2bdea2ebee948e32359f5598e98a7cd4}\label{namespaceflatbuffers_a2bdea2ebee948e32359f5598e98a7cd4} 
\index{flatbuffers@{flatbuffers}!hash\_value\_t@{hash\_value\_t}}
\index{hash\_value\_t@{hash\_value\_t}!flatbuffers@{flatbuffers}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{hash\_value\_t}{hash\_value\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef uint64\+\_\+t \mbox{\hyperlink{namespaceflatbuffers_a2bdea2ebee948e32359f5598e98a7cd4}{flatbuffers\+::hash\+\_\+value\+\_\+t}}}



Function types to be used with resolving hashes into objects and back again. The resolver gets a pointer to a field inside an object API object that is of the type specified in the schema using the attribute {\ttfamily cpp\+\_\+type} (it is thus important whatever you write to this address matches that type). The value of this field is initially null, so you may choose to implement a delayed binding lookup using this function if you wish. The resolver does the opposite lookup, for when the object is being serialized again.

This can compute the start of a Flat\+Buffer from a root pointer, i.\+e. it is the opposite transformation of Get\+Root(). This may be useful if you want to pass on a root and have the recipient delete the buffer afterwards.
